I've uploaded a code repository in the directory /testbed. Consider the following PR description:

<pr_description>
Animated graphic doesn't invalidate parent AVM2Button's cached bitmap
### Describe the bug

Consider the Play button from #11907: [BurgeriaMenuButtons.zip](https://github.com/ruffle-rs/ruffle/files/11954572/BurgeriaMenuButtons.zip)
The idle/attract highlight animation has a noticeable pause in the middle:
![ruffle_BurgeriaPlayButton](https://github.com/ruffle-rs/ruffle/assets/71368227/9922d47f-5231-4ec0-a816-81b5328ce869)

Here is a simplified project with frames added to the animation to make it even more obvious: [BurgeriaPlayButtonNoBlend.zip](https://github.com/ruffle-rs/ruffle/files/13997160/BurgeriaPlayButtonNoBlend.zip)

Notice also that the pause does not happen in the SWF from #14858. This is because the problem only affects AVM2Button, not AVM1Button. The button has Cache as Bitmap enabled, and each frame of the animation should invalidate the parent button's bitmap cache, but this is not happening in AVM2Button.

### Expected behavior

The idle/attract animation should play smoothly:
![flashplayer_BurgeriaPlayButton](https://github.com/ruffle-rs/ruffle/assets/71368227/3c1cbaf6-0e46-4a6d-b119-caac840100f7)


### Content Location

Original project: [BurgeriaMenuButtons.zip](https://github.com/ruffle-rs/ruffle/files/11954572/BurgeriaMenuButtons.zip)
Simplified project: [BurgeriaPlayButtonNoBlend.zip](https://github.com/ruffle-rs/ruffle/files/13997160/BurgeriaPlayButtonNoBlend.zip)

### Affected platform

Desktop app

### Operating system

Windows 10

### Browser

_No response_

### Additional information

Possibly related to #14755.

</pr_description>

   823	    /// This may only be called once per frame - the first call will return true, regardless of
   824	    /// if there was a cache.
   825	    /// Any subsequent calls will return false, indicating that you do not need to invalidate the ancestors.

   827	    fn invalidate_cached_bitmap(&self) -> bool {
   828	        if self.contains_flag(DisplayObjectFlags::CACHE_INVALIDATED) {
   829	            return false;
   830	        }

   832	            cache.make_dirty();

   835	        true
   836	    }

    66	    pub fn from_swf_tag(button: &swf::Button, source_movie: &SwfSlice, mc: &Mutation<'gc>) -> Self {
    67	        let actions = button
    68	            .actions
    69	            .iter()
    70	            .map(|action| ButtonAction {
    71	                action_data: source_movie.to_unbounded_subslice(action.action_data),
    72	                conditions: action.conditions,
    73	            })
    74	            .collect();
    75	
    76	        Avm1Button(Gc::new(
    77	            mc,
    78	            Avm1ButtonData {
    79	                base: Default::default(),
    80	                cell: RefLock::new(Avm1ButtonDataMut {
    81	                    container: ChildContainer::new(&source_movie.movie),
    82	                    hit_area: BTreeMap::new(),
    83	                    hit_bounds: Default::default(),
    84	                    text_field_bindings: Vec::new(),
    85	                }),
    86	                shared: Gc::new(
    87	                    mc,
    88	                    ButtonShared {
    89	                        swf: source_movie.movie.clone(),
    90	                        id: button.id,
    91	                        actions,
    92	                        cell: RefCell::new(ButtonSharedMut {
    93	                            records: button.records.clone(),
    94	                            up_to_over_sound: None,
    95	                            over_to_down_sound: None,
    96	                            down_to_over_sound: None,
    97	                            over_to_up_sound: None,
    98	                        }),
    99	                    },
   100	                ),
   101	                state: Cell::new(ButtonState::Up),
   102	                initialized: Cell::new(false),
   103	                object: Lock::new(None),
   104	                tracking: Cell::new(if button.is_track_as_menu {
   105	                    ButtonTracking::Menu
   106	                } else {
   107	                    ButtonTracking::Push
   108	                }),
   109	            },
   110	        ))
   111	    }

   113	    pub fn set_sounds(self, sounds: swf::ButtonSounds) {
   114	        let mut shared = self.0.shared.cell.borrow_mut();
   115	        shared.up_to_over_sound = sounds.up_to_over_sound;
   116	        shared.over_to_down_sound = sounds.over_to_down_sound;
   117	        shared.down_to_over_sound = sounds.down_to_over_sound;
   118	        shared.over_to_up_sound = sounds.over_to_up_sound;

   121	    /// Handles the ancient DefineButtonCxform SWF tag.
   122	    /// Set the color transform for all children of each state.
   123	    pub fn set_colors(self, color_transforms: &[swf::ColorTransform]) {
   124	        let mut shared = self.0.shared.cell.borrow_mut();
   125	
   126	        // This tag isn't documented well in SWF19. It is only used in very old SWF<=2 content.
   127	        // It applies color transforms to every character in a button, in sequence(?).
   128	        for (record, color_transform) in shared.records.iter_mut().zip(color_transforms.iter()) {
   129	            record.color_transform = *color_transform;
   130	        }
   131	    }
   132	
   133	    /// Set the state of a button, creating or destroying children as needed.
   134	    ///
   135	    /// This function instantiates children and thus must not be called whilst
   136	    /// the caller is holding a write lock on the button data.
   137	    pub fn set_state(mut self, context: &mut UpdateContext<'gc>, state: ButtonState) {
   138	        let mut removed_depths: fnv::FnvHashSet<_> =
   139	            self.iter_render_list().map(|o| o.depth()).collect();
   140	
   141	        let movie = self.movie();
   142	        self.0.state.set(state);
   143	
   144	        // Create any new children that exist in this state, and remove children
   145	        // that only exist in the previous state.
   146	        // Children that exist in both states should persist and not be recreated.
   147	        // TODO: This behavior probably differs in AVM2 (I suspect they always get recreated).
   148	        let mut children = Vec::new();
   149	
   150	        for record in &self.0.shared.cell.borrow().records {
   151	            if record.states.contains(state.into()) {
   152	                // State contains this depth, so we don't have to remove it.
   153	                removed_depths.remove(&record.depth.into());
   154	
   155	                let child = match self.child_by_depth(record.depth.into()) {
   156	                    // Re-use existing child.
   157	                    Some(child) if child.id() == record.id => child,
   158	
   159	                    // Instantiate new child.
   160	                    _ => {
   161	                        if let Some(child) = context
   162	                            .library
   163	                            .library_for_movie_mut(movie.clone())
   164	                            .instantiate_by_id(record.id, context.gc_context)
   165	                        {
   166	                            // New child that did not previously exist, create it.
   167	                            child.set_parent(context, Some(self.into()));
   168	                            child.set_depth(record.depth.into());
   169	
   170	                            children.push((child, record.depth));
   171	                            child
   172	                        } else {
   173	                            continue;
   174	                        }
   175	                    }
   176	                };
   177	
   178	                // Set transform of child (and modify previous child if it already existed)
   179	                child.set_matrix(record.matrix.into());
   180	                child.set_color_transform(record.color_transform);
   181	                child.set_blend_mode(record.blend_mode.into());
   182	                child.set_filters(record.filters.iter().map(Filter::from).collect());
   183	            }
   184	        }
   185	
   186	        // Kill children that no longer exist in this state.
   187	        for depth in removed_depths {
   188	            if let Some(child) = self.child_by_depth(depth) {
   189	                self.remove_child(context, child);
   190	            }
   191	        }
   192	
   193	        for (child, depth) in children {
   194	            // Initialize new child.
   195	            child.post_instantiation(context, None, Instantiator::Movie, false);
   196	            if let Some(clip) = child.as_movie_clip() {
   197	                clip.run_frame_avm1(context);
   198	            }
   199	            let removed_child = self.replace_at_depth(context, child, depth.into());
   200	            dispatch_added_event(self.into(), child, false, context);
   201	            if let Some(removed_child) = removed_child {
   202	                dispatch_removed_event(removed_child, context);
   203	            }
   204	        }
   205	
   206	        self.invalidate_cached_bitmap();
   207	    }
   208	
   209	    pub fn state(self) -> Option<ButtonState> {
   210	        Some(self.0.state.get())
   211	    }
   212	
   213	    fn get_boolean_property(
   214	        self,
   215	        name: AvmString<'gc>,
   216	        default: bool,
   217	        context: &mut UpdateContext<'gc>,
   218	    ) -> bool {
   219	        if let Some(object) = self.object1() {
   220	            let mut activation = Activation::from_nothing(
   221	                context,
   222	                ActivationIdentifier::root("[AVM1 Boolean Property]"),
   223	                self.avm1_root(),
   224	            );
   225	            if let Ok(value) = object.get(name, &mut activation) {
   226	                match value {
   227	                    Value::Undefined => default,
   228	                    _ => value.as_bool(activation.swf_version()),
   229	                }
   230	            } else {
   231	                default
   232	            }
   233	        } else {
   234	            false
   235	        }
   236	    }

   240	    }

   405	impl<'gc> TInteractiveObject<'gc> for Avm1Button<'gc> {
   406	    fn raw_interactive(self) -> Gc<'gc, InteractiveObjectBase<'gc>> {
   407	        HasPrefixField::as_prefix_gc(self.0)
   408	    }
   409	
   410	    fn as_displayobject(self) -> DisplayObject<'gc> {
   411	        self.into()
   412	    }
   413	
   414	    fn filter_clip_event(
   415	        self,
   416	        _context: &mut UpdateContext<'gc>,
   417	        event: ClipEvent,
   418	    ) -> ClipEventResult {
   419	        // An invisible button can still run its `rollOut` or `releaseOutside` event.
   420	        // A disabled button doesn't run its events (`KeyPress` being the exception) but
   421	        // its state can still change. This is tested at "avm1/mouse_events_visible_enabled".
   422	        if !self.visible() && self.0.state.get() == ButtonState::Up {
   423	            return ClipEventResult::NotHandled;
   424	        }
   425	
   426	        // The `keyPress` event doesn't fire if the button is inside another button.
   427	        if matches!(event, ClipEvent::KeyPress { .. })
   428	            && self.parent().and_then(|p| p.as_avm1_button()).is_some()
   429	        {
   430	            return ClipEventResult::NotHandled;
   431	        }
   432	
   433	        ClipEventResult::Handled
   434	    }
   435	
   436	    fn event_dispatch(self, context: &mut UpdateContext<'gc>, event: ClipEvent) -> ClipEventResult {
   437	        let self_display_object = self.into();
   438	        let is_enabled = self.enabled(context);
   439	
   440	        // Translate the clip event to a button event, based on how the button state changes.
   441	        let shared = self.0.shared;
   442	        let shared = shared.cell.borrow();
   443	        let (new_state, condition, sound) = match event {
   444	            ClipEvent::DragOut { .. } => (
   445	                ButtonState::Over,
   446	                Some(ButtonActionCondition::OVER_DOWN_TO_OUT_DOWN),
   447	                None,
   448	            ),
   449	            ClipEvent::DragOver { .. } => (
   450	                ButtonState::Down,
   451	                Some(ButtonActionCondition::OUT_DOWN_TO_OVER_DOWN),
   452	                None,
   453	            ),
   454	            ClipEvent::Press { .. } => (
   455	                ButtonState::Down,
   456	                Some(ButtonActionCondition::OVER_UP_TO_OVER_DOWN),
   457	                shared.over_to_down_sound.as_ref(),
   458	            ),
   459	            ClipEvent::Release { .. } => (
   460	                ButtonState::Over,
   461	                Some(ButtonActionCondition::OVER_DOWN_TO_OVER_UP),
   462	                shared.down_to_over_sound.as_ref(),
   463	            ),
   464	            ClipEvent::ReleaseOutside => (
   465	                ButtonState::Up,
   466	                Some(ButtonActionCondition::OUT_DOWN_TO_IDLE),
   467	                shared.over_to_up_sound.as_ref(),
   468	            ),
   469	            ClipEvent::RollOut { .. } => (
   470	                ButtonState::Up,
   471	                Some(ButtonActionCondition::OVER_UP_TO_IDLE),
   472	                shared.over_to_up_sound.as_ref(),
   473	            ),
   474	            ClipEvent::RollOver { .. } => (
   475	                ButtonState::Over,
   476	                Some(ButtonActionCondition::IDLE_TO_OVER_UP),
   477	                shared.up_to_over_sound.as_ref(),
   478	            ),
   479	            ClipEvent::KeyPress { key_code } => {
   480	                return self.0.run_actions(
   481	                    context,
   482	                    ButtonActionCondition::from_key_code(key_code.to_u8()),
   483	                );
   484	            }
   485	            // KeyUp and KeyDown might fire some event handlers
   486	            ClipEvent::KeyUp => (self.0.state.get(), None, None),
   487	            ClipEvent::KeyDown => (self.0.state.get(), None, None),
   488	            _ => return ClipEventResult::NotHandled,
   489	        };
   490	
   491	        let (update_state, new_state) = if is_enabled {
   492	            if let Some(condition) = condition {
   493	                self.0.run_actions(context, condition);
   494	            }
   495	            if let Some((id, sound_info)) = sound {
   496	                AudioManager::perform_sound_event(self.into(), context, *id, sound_info);
   497	            }
   498	
   499	            // Queue ActionScript-defined event handlers after the SWF defined ones.
   500	            // (e.g., clip.onRelease = foo).
   501	            if self.should_fire_event_handlers(context, event)
   502	                && let Some(name) = event.method_name(&context.strings)
   503	            {
   504	                context.action_queue.queue_action(
   505	                    self_display_object,
   506	                    ActionType::Method {
   507	                        object: self.0.object.get().unwrap(),
   508	                        name,
   509	                        args: vec![],
   510	                    },
   511	                    false,
   512	                );
   513	            }
   514	
   515	            (self.0.state.get() != new_state, new_state)
   516	        } else {
   517	            // Remove the current mouse hovered and mouse down objects.
   518	            // This is required to make sure the button will fire its events if it gets enabled.
   519	            if InteractiveObject::option_ptr_eq(Some(self.into()), context.mouse_data.hovered) {
   520	                context.mouse_data.hovered = None;

    48	pub struct Avm2ButtonData<'gc> {

    90	    ///
    91	    /// This flag exists due to a really odd feature of buttons: they run their

    93	    /// normal AVM2 execution order for future frames.

   102	impl<'gc> Avm2Button<'gc> {
   103	    pub fn from_swf_tag(
   104	        button: &swf::Button,
   105	        source_movie: &SwfSlice,
   106	        context: &mut UpdateContext<'gc>,
   107	        construct_blank_states: bool,
   108	    ) -> Self {
   109	        Avm2Button(Gc::new(
   110	            context.gc(),
   111	            Avm2ButtonData {
   112	                base: Default::default(),
   113	                shared: Gc::new(
   114	                    context.gc(),
   115	                    ButtonShared {
   116	                        swf: source_movie.movie.clone(),
   117	                        id: button.id,
   118	                        cell: RefCell::new(ButtonSharedMut {
   119	                            records: button.records.clone(),
   120	                            up_to_over_sound: None,
   121	                            over_to_down_sound: None,
   122	                            down_to_over_sound: None,
   123	                            over_to_up_sound: None,
   124	                        }),
   125	                    },
   126	                ),
   127	                state: Cell::new(self::ButtonState::Up),
   128	                hit_area: Lock::new(None),
   129	                up_state: Lock::new(None),
   130	                over_state: Lock::new(None),
   131	                down_state: Lock::new(None),
   132	                class: Lock::new(context.avm2.classes().simplebutton),
   133	                object: Lock::new(None),
   134	                needs_frame_construction: Cell::new(construct_blank_states),
   135	                tracking: Cell::new(if button.is_track_as_menu {
   136	                    ButtonTracking::Menu
   137	                } else {
   138	                    ButtonTracking::Push
   139	                }),
   140	                enabled: Cell::new(true),
   141	                use_hand_cursor: Cell::new(true),
   142	                skip_current_frame: Cell::new(false),
   143	                weird_framescript_order: Cell::new(false),
   144	            },
   145	        ))
   146	    }
   147	
   148	    pub fn empty_button(context: &mut UpdateContext<'gc>) -> Self {
   149	        let movie = context.root_swf.clone();
   150	        let button_record = swf::Button {
   151	            id: 0,
   152	            is_track_as_menu: false,
   153	            records: Vec::new(),
   154	            actions: Vec::new(),
   155	        };
   156	
   157	        Self::from_swf_tag(&button_record, &movie.into(), context, false)
   158	    }
   159	
   160	    pub fn set_sounds(self, sounds: swf::ButtonSounds) {
   161	        let mut shared = self.0.shared.cell.borrow_mut();
   162	        shared.up_to_over_sound = sounds.up_to_over_sound;
   163	        shared.over_to_down_sound = sounds.over_to_down_sound;
   164	        shared.down_to_over_sound = sounds.down_to_over_sound;
   165	        shared.over_to_up_sound = sounds.over_to_up_sound;
   166	    }
   167	
   168	    /// Handles the ancient DefineButtonCxform SWF tag.
   169	    /// Set the color transform for all children of each state.
   170	    pub fn set_colors(self, color_transforms: &[swf::ColorTransform]) {
   171	        let mut shared = self.0.shared.cell.borrow_mut();
   172	
   173	        // This tag isn't documented well in SWF19. It is only used in very old SWF<=2 content.
   174	        // It applies color transforms to every character in a button, in sequence(?).
   175	        for (record, color_transform) in shared.records.iter_mut().zip(color_transforms.iter()) {
   176	            record.color_transform = *color_transform;
   177	        }
   178	    }
   179	
   180	    /// Construct a given state of the button and return it's containing
   181	    /// DisplayObject.
   182	    ///
   183	    /// In contrast to AVM1Button, the AVM2 variety constructs all of it's
   184	    /// children once and stores them in four named slots, either on their own
   185	    /// (if they are singular) or in `Sprite`s created specifically to store
   186	    /// button children. This means that, for example, a child that exists in
   187	    /// multiple states in the SWF will actually be instantiated multiple
   188	    /// times.
   189	    ///
   190	    /// If the boolean parameter is `true`, then the caller of this function
   191	    /// should signal events on all children of the returned display object.
   192	    fn create_state(
   193	        self,
   194	        context: &mut UpdateContext<'gc>,
   195	        swf_state: swf::ButtonState,
   196	    ) -> (DisplayObject<'gc>, bool) {
   197	        let movie = self.movie();
   198	        let sprite_class = context.avm2.classes().sprite;
   199	
   200	        let mut children = Vec::new();
   201	        let shared = self.0.shared;
   202	
   203	        for record in shared.cell.borrow().records.iter() {
   204	            if record.states.contains(swf_state) {
   205	                match context
   206	                    .library
   207	                    .library_for_movie_mut(movie.clone())
   208	                    .instantiate_by_id(record.id, context.gc_context)
   209	                {
   210	                    Some(child) => {
   211	                        child.set_matrix(record.matrix.into());
   212	                        child.set_depth(record.depth.into());
   213	
   214	                        if swf_state != swf::ButtonState::HIT_TEST {
   215	                            child.set_color_transform(record.color_transform);
   216	                            child.set_blend_mode(record.blend_mode.into());
   217	                            child.set_filters(record.filters.iter().map(Filter::from).collect());
   218	                        }
   219	
   220	                        children.push((child, record.depth));
   221	                    }
   222	                    None => {
   223	                        tracing::error!(
   224	                            "Button ID {}: could not instantiate child ID {}",
   225	                            shared.id,
   226	                            record.id,
   227	                        );
   228	                    }
   229	                };
   230	            }
   231	        }
   232	
   233	        self.invalidate_cached_bitmap();
   234	
   235	        // We manually call `construct_frame` for `child` and `state_sprite` - normally
   236	        // this would be done in the `DisplayObject` constructor, but SimpleButton does
   237	        // not have children in the normal DisplayObjectContainer sense.
   238	
   239	        if children.len() == 1 {
   240	            let child = children.first().cloned().unwrap().0;
   241	
   242	            child.set_parent(context, Some(self.into()));
   243	            child.post_instantiation(context, None, Instantiator::Movie, false);
   244	            catchup_display_object_to_frame(context, child);
   245	            child.construct_frame(context);
   246	
   247	            (child, false)
   248	        } else {
   249	            let state_sprite = MovieClip::new(movie, context.gc());
   250	            state_sprite.set_avm2_class(context.gc(), Some(sprite_class));
   251	            state_sprite.set_parent(context, Some(self.into()));
   252	            catchup_display_object_to_frame(context, state_sprite.into());
   253	
   254	            for (child, depth) in children {
   255	                // `parent` returns `null` for these grandchildren during construction time, even though
   256	                // `stage` and `root` will be defined. Set the parent temporarily to the button itself so
   257	                // that `parent` is `null` (`DisplayObject::avm2_parent` checks that the parent is a container),
   258	                // and then properly set the parent to the state Sprite afterwards.
   259	                state_sprite.replace_at_depth(context, child, depth.into());
   260	                child.set_parent(context, Some(self.into()));
   261	                child.post_instantiation(context, None, Instantiator::Movie, false);
   262	                catchup_display_object_to_frame(context, child);
   263	                child.set_parent(context, Some(state_sprite.into()));
   264	                child.construct_frame(context);
   265	            }
   266	
   267	            state_sprite.construct_frame(context);
   268	
   269	            (state_sprite.into(), true)
   270	        }
   271	    }
   272	
   273	    /// Get the rendered state of the button.
   274	    pub fn state(self) -> ButtonState {
   275	        self.0.state.get()
   276	    }
   277	
   278	    /// Change the rendered state of the button.
   279	    pub fn set_state(self, context: &mut UpdateContext<'gc>, state: ButtonState) {
   280	        self.invalidate_cached_bitmap();
   281	        self.0.state.set(state);
   282	
   283	        for state in self.all_state_children(false) {
   284	            state.set_parent(context, None);
   285	        }
   286	        if let Some(state) = self.get_state_child(state.into()) {
   287	            state.set_parent(context, Some(self.into()));
   288	        }
   289	    }
   290	
   291	    /// Get all the display objects representing button states.
   292	    fn all_state_children(
   293	        &self,
   294	        weird_order: bool,
   295	    ) -> impl Iterator<Item = DisplayObject<'gc>> + '_ {
   296	        let children = if weird_order {
   297	            [
   298	                &self.0.up_state,
   299	                &self.0.over_state,
   300	                &self.0.down_state,
   301	                &self.0.hit_area,
   302	            ]
   303	        } else {
   304	            [
   305	                &self.0.hit_area,
   306	                &self.0.up_state,
   307	                &self.0.down_state,
   308	                &self.0.over_state,
   309	            ]
   310	        };
   311	        children.into_iter().filter_map(Lock::get)
   312	    }
   313	
   314	    /// Get the display object that represents a particular button state.
   315	    pub fn get_state_child(self, state: swf::ButtonState) -> Option<DisplayObject<'gc>> {
   316	        match state {
   317	            swf::ButtonState::UP => self.0.up_state.get(),
   318	            swf::ButtonState::OVER => self.0.over_state.get(),
   319	            swf::ButtonState::DOWN => self.0.down_state.get(),
   320	            swf::ButtonState::HIT_TEST => self.0.hit_area.get(),
   321	            _ => None,
   322	        }
   323	    }
   324	
   325	    /// Set the display object that represents a particular button state.
   326	    pub fn set_state_child(
   327	        self,
   328	        context: &mut UpdateContext<'gc>,
   329	        state: swf::ButtonState,
   330	        child: Option<DisplayObject<'gc>>,
   331	    ) {
   332	        let child_was_on_stage = child.map(|c| c.is_on_stage(context)).unwrap_or(false);
   333	        let old_state_child = self.get_state_child(state);
   334	        let is_cur_state = swf::ButtonState::from(self.0.state.get()) == state;
   335	
   336	        let write = Gc::write(context.gc(), self.0);
   337	        match state {
   338	            swf::ButtonState::UP => unlock!(write, Avm2ButtonData, up_state).set(child),
   339	            swf::ButtonState::OVER => unlock!(write, Avm2ButtonData, over_state).set(child),
   340	            swf::ButtonState::DOWN => unlock!(write, Avm2ButtonData, down_state).set(child),
   341	            swf::ButtonState::HIT_TEST => unlock!(write, Avm2ButtonData, hit_area).set(child),
   342	            _ => (),
   343	        }
   344	
   345	        if let Some(child) = child {
   346	            if let Some(mut parent) = child.parent().and_then(|parent| parent.as_container()) {
   347	                parent.remove_child(context, child);
   348	            }
   349	
   350	            if is_cur_state {
   351	                child.set_parent(context, Some(self.into()));
   352	            }
   353	        }
   354	
   355	        if let Some(old_state_child) = old_state_child {
   356	            old_state_child.set_parent(context, None);
   357	        }
   358	
   359	        if is_cur_state {
   360	            if let Some(child) = child {
   361	                dispatch_added_event(self.into(), child, child_was_on_stage, context);
   362	            }
   363	
   364	            if let Some(old_state_child) = old_state_child {
   365	                dispatch_removed_event(old_state_child, context);
   366	            }
   367	
   368	            // FIXME is this correct?
   369	            if child.is_some() {
   370	                broadcast_frame_constructed(context);
   371	            }
   372	        }
   373	
   374	        if is_cur_state && let Some(child) = child {
   375	            child.run_frame_scripts(context);
   376	            // FIXME is this correct?
   377	            broadcast_frame_exited(context);
   378	        }
   379	    }
   380	
   381	    pub fn enabled(self) -> bool {
   382	        self.0.enabled.get()
   383	    }

   446	    fn construct_frame(self, context: &mut UpdateContext<'gc>) {
   447	        for state in self.all_state_children(false) {
   448	            state.construct_frame(context);
   449	        }
   450

   456	                let object_cell = unlock!(Gc::write(context.gc(), self.0), Avm2ButtonData, object);

   458	                object_cell.set(Some(object));

   461	                    // This is run before we actually call the constructor - the un-constructed object
   462	                    // is exposed to ActionScript via `parent.<childName>`.
   463	                    self.set_on_parent_field(context);
   464	                }
   465	            }

   467	            // Prevent re-entrantly constructing this button (since we may run a nested frame here)
   468	            self.0.needs_frame_construction.set(false);

   471	            let (down_state, down_should_fire) = self.create_state(context, swf::ButtonState::DOWN);

   519	                // which means that `self` can't have listeners set yet,

   577	    fn self_bounds(self, _mode: BoundsMode) -> Rectangle<Twips> {
   578	        // No inherent bounds; contains child DisplayObjects.
   579	        Default::default()
   580	    }
   581	
   582	    fn bounds_with_transform(self, matrix: &Matrix, mode: BoundsMode) -> Rectangle<Twips> {
   583	        // A scroll rect completely overrides an object's bounds,
   584	        // and can even grow the bounding box to be larger than the actual content
   585	        if let Some(scroll_rect) = self.scroll_rect() {
   586	            return *matrix
   587	                * Rectangle {
   588	                    x_min: Twips::ZERO,
   589	                    y_min: Twips::ZERO,
   590	                    x_max: scroll_rect.width(),
   591	                    y_max: scroll_rect.height(),
   592	                };
   593	        }
   594	
   595	        // Get self bounds
   596	        let mut bounds = *matrix * self.self_bounds(mode);
   597	
   598	        // Add the bounds of the child, dictated by current state
   599	        if let Some(child) = self.get_state_child(self.0.state.get().into()) {
   600	            let matrix = *matrix * child.base().matrix();
   601	            let child_bounds = child.bounds_with_transform(&matrix, mode);
   602	            bounds = bounds.union(&child_bounds);
   603	        }
   604	
   605	        bounds
   606	    }
   607	
   608	    fn render_bounds_with_transform(
   609	        self,
   610	        matrix: &Matrix,
   611	        include_own_filters: bool,
   612	        view_matrix: &Matrix,
   613	    ) -> Rectangle<Twips> {
   614	        let mut bounds = *matrix * self.self_bounds(BoundsMode::Engine);
   615	
   616	        if let Some(child) = self.get_state_child(self.0.state.get().into()) {
   617	            let matrix = *matrix * child.base().matrix();
   618	            bounds = bounds.union(&child.render_bounds_with_transform(&matrix, true, view_matrix));
   619	        }
   620	
   621	        if include_own_filters {
   622	            for mut filter in self.filters().iter().cloned() {
   623	                filter.scale(view_matrix.a, view_matrix.d);
   624	                bounds = filter.calculate_dest_rect(bounds);
   625	            }
   626	        }
   627	
   628	        bounds
   629	    }
   630	
   631	    fn hit_test_shape(
   632	        self,
   633	        context: &mut UpdateContext<'gc>,
   634	        point: Point<Twips>,
   635	        options: HitTestOptions,
   636	    ) -> bool {
   637	        if (!options.contains(HitTestOptions::SKIP_INVISIBLE) || self.visible())
   638	            && let Some(child) = self.get_state_child(self.0.state.get().into())
   639	        {
   640	            //TODO: the if below should probably always be taken, why does the hit area
   641	            // sometimes have a parent?
   642	            let mut point = point;
   643	            if child.parent().is_none() {
   644	                // hit_area is not actually a child, so transform point into local space before passing it down.
   645	                point = if let Some(point) = self.global_to_local(point) {
   646	                    point
   647	                } else {
   648	                    return false;
   649	                }
   650	            }
   651	
   652	            if child.hit_test_shape(context, point, options) {
   653	                return true;
   654	            }
   655	        }
   656	
   657	        false
   658	    }

   693	    fn filter_clip_event(
   694	        self,
   695	        _context: &mut UpdateContext<'gc>,
   696	        event: ClipEvent,
   697	    ) -> ClipEventResult {
   698	        if !self.visible() {
   699	            return ClipEventResult::NotHandled;
   700	        }
   701	
   702	        if !self.enabled() && !matches!(event, ClipEvent::KeyPress { .. }) {
   703	            return ClipEventResult::NotHandled;
   704	        }
   705	
   706	        ClipEventResult::Handled
   707	    }
   708	
   709	    fn propagate_to_children(
   710	        self,
   711	        context: &mut UpdateContext<'gc>,
   712	        event: ClipEvent<'gc>,
   713	    ) -> ClipEventResult {
   714	        if event.propagates() {
   715	            let current_state = self.get_state_child(self.0.state.get().into());
   716	
   717	            if let Some(current_state) = current_state.and_then(|s| s.as_interactive())
   718	                && current_state.handle_clip_event(context, event) == ClipEventResult::Handled
   719	            {
   720	                return ClipEventResult::Handled;
   721	            }
   722	        }
   723	
   724	        ClipEventResult::NotHandled
   725	    }
   726	
   727	    fn event_dispatch(
   728	        self,
   729	        context: &mut UpdateContext<'gc>,
   730	        event: ClipEvent<'gc>,
   731	    ) -> ClipEventResult {
   732	        // Translate the clip event to a button event, based on how the button state changes.
   733	        let shared = self.0.shared.cell.borrow();
   734	        let (new_state, sound) = match event {
   735	            ClipEvent::DragOut { .. } => (ButtonState::Over, None),
   736	            ClipEvent::DragOver { .. } => (ButtonState::Down, None),
   737	            ClipEvent::Press { .. } => (ButtonState::Down, shared.over_to_down_sound.as_ref()),
   738	            ClipEvent::Release { .. } => (ButtonState::Over, shared.down_to_over_sound.as_ref()),
   739	            ClipEvent::ReleaseOutside => (ButtonState::Up, shared.over_to_up_sound.as_ref()),
   740	            ClipEvent::MouseUpInside => (ButtonState::Up, shared.over_to_up_sound.as_ref()),

   727	    fn event_dispatch(
   728	        self,
   729	        context: &mut UpdateContext<'gc>,
   730	        event: ClipEvent<'gc>,
   731	    ) -> ClipEventResult {
   732	        // Translate the clip event to a button event, based on how the button state changes.
   733	        let shared = self.0.shared.cell.borrow();
   734	        let (new_state, sound) = match event {
   735	            ClipEvent::DragOut { .. } => (ButtonState::Over, None),
   736	            ClipEvent::DragOver { .. } => (ButtonState::Down, None),
   737	            ClipEvent::Press { .. } => (ButtonState::Down, shared.over_to_down_sound.as_ref()),
   738	            ClipEvent::Release { .. } => (ButtonState::Over, shared.down_to_over_sound.as_ref()),
   739	            ClipEvent::ReleaseOutside => (ButtonState::Up, shared.over_to_up_sound.as_ref()),
   740	            ClipEvent::MouseUpInside => (ButtonState::Up, shared.over_to_up_sound.as_ref()),
   741	            ClipEvent::RollOut { .. } => (ButtonState::Up, shared.over_to_up_sound.as_ref()),
   742	            ClipEvent::RollOver { .. } => (ButtonState::Over, shared.up_to_over_sound.as_ref()),
   743	            _ => return ClipEventResult::NotHandled,
   744	        };

   747	            AudioManager::perform_sound_event(self.into(), context, *id, sound_info);
   748	        }
   749	        let old_state = self.0.state.get();
   750	
   751	        if old_state != new_state {
   752	            self.set_state(context, new_state);
   753	        }
   754	        ClipEventResult::Handled
   755	    }

   757	    fn mouse_pick_avm2(
   758	        self,
   759	        context: &mut UpdateContext<'gc>,
   760	        mut point: Point<Twips>,
   761	        require_button_mode: bool,
   762	    ) -> Avm2MousePick<'gc> {
   763	        // The button is hovered if the mouse is over any child nodes.
   764	        if self.visible() && self.mouse_enabled() {
   765	            let state_child = self.get_state_child(self.0.state.get().into());
   766	
   767	            if let Some(state_child) = state_child {
   768	                let mouse_pick = state_child
   769	                    .as_interactive()
   770	                    .map(|c| c.mouse_pick_avm2(context, point, require_button_mode));
   771	                match mouse_pick {
   772	                    None | Some(Avm2MousePick::Miss) => {}
   773	                    // Selecting a child of a button is equivalent to selecting the button itself
   774	                    _ => return Avm2MousePick::Hit(self.into()),
   775	                };
   776	            }
   777	
   778	            if let Some(hit_area) = self.0.hit_area.get() {
   779	                //TODO: the if below should probably always be taken, why does the hit area
   780	                // sometimes have a parent?
   781	                if hit_area.parent().is_none() {
   782	                    // hit_area is not actually a child, so transform point into local space before passing it down.
   783	                    point = if let Some(point) = self.global_to_local(point) {
   784	                        point
   785	                    } else {
   786	                        return Avm2MousePick::Miss;
   787	                    }
   788	                }
   789	                if hit_area.hit_test_shape(context, point, HitTestOptions::MOUSE_PICK) {
   790	                    return Avm2MousePick::Hit(self.into());
   791	                }
   792	            }
   793	        }
   794	        Avm2MousePick::Miss
   795	    }
   796	
   797	    fn mouse_cursor(self, _context: &mut UpdateContext<'gc>) -> MouseCursor {
   798	        // TODO: Should we also need to check for the `enabled` property like AVM1 buttons?
   799	        if self.use_hand_cursor() {
   800	            MouseCursor::Hand
   801	        } else {
   802	            MouseCursor::Arrow
   803	        }
   804	    }
   805	
   806	    fn tab_enabled_default(self, _context: &mut UpdateContext<'gc>) -> bool {
   807	        true
   808	    }
   809	
   810	    fn highlight_bounds(self) -> Rectangle<Twips> {
   811	        let hit_area = self.0.hit_area.get();
   812	        let hit_bounds = hit_area
   813	            .map(|hit| hit.bounds(BoundsMode::Engine))
   814	            .unwrap_or(Rectangle::INVALID);
   815	        self.local_to_global_matrix() * hit_bounds
   816	    }
   817	}

   148	        if self.movie().is_action_script_3() && self.object2().is_none() {
   149	            let class_object = self
   150	                .0
   151	                .class
   152	                .get()
   153	                .unwrap_or_else(|| context.avm2.classes().shape);
   154

   170	                }

   172

   174	        }
   175	    }

   177	    fn replace_with(self, context: &mut UpdateContext<'gc>, id: CharacterId) {
   178	        // Static assets like Graphics can replace themselves via a PlaceObject tag with PlaceObjectAction::Replace.
   179	        // This does not create a new instance, but instead swaps out the underlying static data to point to the new art.
   180	        if let Some(new_graphic) = context
   181	            .library
   182	            .library_for_movie_mut(self.movie())
   183	            .get_graphic(id)

   185	            self.set_shared(context.gc(), new_graphic.0.shared.get());
   186	        } else {
   187	            tracing::warn!("PlaceObject: expected Graphic at character ID {}", id);
   188	        }
   189	        self.invalidate_cached_bitmap();
   190	    }

   192	    fn render_self(self, context: &mut RenderContext) {
   193	        if !context.is_offscreen
   194	            && !self
   195	                .world_bounds(BoundsMode::Engine)
   196	                .intersects(&context.stage.view_bounds())
   197	        {
   198	            // Off-screen; culled
   199	            return;
   200	        }
   201	
   202	        if let Some(drawing) = self.0.drawing.get() {
   203	            drawing.borrow().render(context);
   204	        } else if let Some(render_handle) = self.0.shared.get().render_handle.clone() {
   205	            context
   206	                .commands
   207	                .render_shape(render_handle, context.transform_stack.transform())
   208	        }
   209	    }
   210	
   211	    fn hit_test_shape(
   212	        self,
   213	        _context: &mut UpdateContext<'gc>,
   214	        point: Point<Twips>,
   215	        options: HitTestOptions,
   216	    ) -> bool {
   217	        // Transform point to local coordinates and test.
   218	        if (!options.contains(HitTestOptions::SKIP_INVISIBLE) || self.visible())
   219	            && self.world_bounds(BoundsMode::Engine).contains(point)
   220	        {
   221	            let Some(local_matrix) = self.global_to_local_matrix() else {
   222	                return false;
   223	            };
   224	            let point = local_matrix * point;
   225	            if let Some(drawing) = self.0.drawing.get() {
   226	                if drawing.borrow().hit_test(point, &local_matrix) {
   227	                    return true;
   228	                }
   229	            } else {
   230	                let shape = &self.0.shared.get().shape;
   231	                return ruffle_render::shape_utils::shape_hit_test(shape, point, &local_matrix);
   232	            }
   233	        }
   234	
   235	        false
   236	    }

  1300	    }
  1301	
  1302	    /// Determine what the clip's next frame should be.
  1303	    fn determine_next_frame(self) -> NextFrame {
  1304	        let mc = self.0.shared.get();
  1305	        // We know that we are not on the last frame if either condition is true:
  1306	        // 1. The movieclip is not done preloading frames (indicated by next_preload_chunk not being u64::MAX)
  1307	        // 2. The current frame is less than the amount of frames loaded.
  1308	        if mc.preload_progress.next_preload_chunk.get() != u64::MAX
  1309	            || self.current_frame() < self.frames_loaded() as u16
  1310	        {
  1311	            NextFrame::Next
  1312	        // The `current_frame` can be larger than `header_frames` if the SWF header
  1313	        // declared fewer frames than we actually have. We only stop the swf if there
  1314	        // was *really* at most a single frame (we declared at most 1 frame, and reached the end
  1315	        // of the stream after executing 0 or 1 frames)
  1316	        } else if self.header_frames() <= 1 && self.current_frame() <= 1 {
  1317	            NextFrame::Same
  1318	        } else {
  1319	            NextFrame::First
  1320	        }
  1321	    }
  1322	
  1323	    fn run_frame_internal(
  1324	        self,
  1325	        context: &mut UpdateContext<'gc>,
  1326	        run_display_actions: bool,
  1327	        run_sounds: bool,
  1328	        is_action_script_3: bool,
  1329	    ) {
  1330	        let shared = Gc::as_ref(self.0.shared.get());
  1331	
  1332	        let next_frame = self.determine_next_frame();
  1333	        match next_frame {
  1334	            NextFrame::Next => {
  1335	                if (self.0.current_frame() + 1) >= shared.preload_progress.cur_preload_frame.get() {
  1336	                    return;
  1337	                }
  1338	
  1339	                // AS3 removals need to happen before frame advance (see below)
  1340	                if !is_action_script_3 {
  1341	                    self.0.increment_current_frame();
  1342	                }
  1343	            }
  1344	            NextFrame::First => return self.run_goto(context, 1, true),
  1345	            NextFrame::Same => self.stop(context),
  1346	        }
  1347	
  1348	        let tag_stream_start = shared.swf.as_ref().as_ptr() as u64;
  1349	        let data = shared.swf.clone();
  1350	        let mut reader = data.read_from(self.0.tag_stream_pos.get());
  1351	
  1352	        let tag_callback = |reader: &mut SwfStream<'_>, tag_code, tag_len| {
  1353	            match tag_code {
  1354	                TagCode::DoAction => self.do_action(context, reader, tag_len),
  1355	                TagCode::PlaceObject if run_display_actions && !is_action_script_3 => {
  1356	                    self.place_object(context, reader, 1)
  1357	                }
  1358	                TagCode::PlaceObject2 if run_display_actions && !is_action_script_3 => {
  1359	                    self.place_object(context, reader, 2)
  1360	                }
  1361	                TagCode::PlaceObject3 if run_display_actions && !is_action_script_3 => {
  1362	                    self.place_object(context, reader, 3)
  1363	                }
  1364	                TagCode::PlaceObject4 if run_display_actions && !is_action_script_3 => {
  1365	                    self.place_object(context, reader, 4)
  1366	                }
  1367	                TagCode::RemoveObject if run_display_actions && !is_action_script_3 => {
  1368	                    self.remove_object(context, reader, 1)
  1369	                }
  1370	                TagCode::RemoveObject2 if run_display_actions && !is_action_script_3 => {
  1371	                    self.remove_object(context, reader, 2)
  1372	                }
  1373	                TagCode::PlaceObject if run_display_actions && is_action_script_3 => {
  1374	                    self.queue_place_object(reader, 1)
  1375	                }
  1376	                TagCode::PlaceObject2 if run_display_actions && is_action_script_3 => {
  1377	                    self.queue_place_object(reader, 2)
  1378	                }
  1379	                TagCode::PlaceObject3 if run_display_actions && is_action_script_3 => {
  1380	                    self.queue_place_object(reader, 3)
  1381	                }
  1382	                TagCode::PlaceObject4 if run_display_actions && is_action_script_3 => {
  1383	                    self.queue_place_object(reader, 4)
  1384	                }
  1385	                TagCode::RemoveObject if run_display_actions && is_action_script_3 => {
  1386	                    self.queue_remove_object(reader, 1)
  1387	                }
  1388	                TagCode::RemoveObject2 if run_display_actions && is_action_script_3 => {
  1389	                    self.queue_remove_object(reader, 2)
  1390	                }
  1391	                TagCode::SetBackgroundColor => self.set_background_color(context, reader),
  1392	                TagCode::StartSound if run_sounds => self.start_sound_1(context, reader),
  1393	                TagCode::SoundStreamBlock if run_sounds => self.sound_stream_block(context, reader),
  1394	                TagCode::ShowFrame => return Ok(ControlFlow::Exit),
  1395	                _ => Ok(()),
  1396	            }?;
  1397	
  1398	            Ok(ControlFlow::Continue)
  1399	        };
  1400	        let _ = tag_utils::decode_tags(&mut reader, tag_callback);
  1401	        if let Err(e) = self.run_abc_and_symbol_tags(context, self.0.current_frame()) {
  1402	            tracing::error!("Error running abc/symbol in frame: {e:?}");
  1403	        }
  1404	
  1405	        // On AS3, we deliberately run all removals before the frame number or
  1406	        // tag position updates. This ensures that code that runs gotos when a
  1407	        // display object is added or removed does not catch the movie clip in
  1408	        // an invalid state.
  1409	        let remove_actions = self.unqueue_filtered(|q| q.unqueue_remove());
  1410	
  1411	        for (_, tag) in remove_actions {
  1412	            let mut reader = data.read_from(tag.tag_start);
  1413	            let version = match tag.tag_type {
  1414	                QueuedTagAction::Remove(v) => v,
  1415	                _ => unreachable!(),
  1416	            };
  1417	
  1418	            if let Err(e) = self.remove_object(context, &mut reader, version) {
  1419	                tracing::error!("Error running queued tag: {:?}, got {}", tag.tag_type, e);
  1420	            }
  1421	        }
  1422	
  1423	        // It is now safe to update the tag position and frame number.
  1424	        // TODO: Determine if explicit gotos override these or not.
  1425	
  1426	        self.0
  1427	            .tag_stream_pos
  1428	            .set(reader.get_ref().as_ptr() as u64 - tag_stream_start);
  1429	
  1430	        // Check if our audio track has finished playing.
  1431	        if let Some(audio_stream) = self.0.audio_stream.get()
  1432	            && !context.is_sound_playing(audio_stream)
  1433	        {
  1434	            self.0.audio_stream.take();
  1435	        }
  1436	
  1437	        if matches!(next_frame, NextFrame::Next) && is_action_script_3 {
  1438	            self.0.increment_current_frame();
  1439	        }
  1440	
  1441	        self.0.queued_script_frame.set(self.0.current_frame.get());
  1442	        if self.last_queued_script_frame() != Some(self.0.current_frame.get()) {
  1443	            // We explicitly clear this variable since AS3 may later GOTO back
  1444	            // to the already-ran frame. Since the frame number *has* changed
  1445	            // in the meantime, it should absolutely run again.
  1446	            self.set_last_queued_script_frame(None);
  1447	        }
  1448	    }
  1449	
  1450	    /// Instantiate a given child object on the timeline at a given depth.
  1451	    fn instantiate_child(
  1452	        self,
  1453	        context: &mut UpdateContext<'gc>,
  1454	        id: CharacterId,
  1455	        depth: Depth,
  1456	        place_object: &swf::PlaceObject,
  1457	    ) -> Option<DisplayObject<'gc>> {
  1458	        if self.has_child_at_depth(depth) {
  1459	            context.avm_warning(&format!("Failed to place object at depth {depth}."));
  1460	            return None;
  1461	        }
  1462	
  1463	        let movie = self.movie();
  1464	        let library = context.library.library_for_movie_mut(movie.clone());
  1465	        match library.instantiate_by_id(id, context.gc_context) {
  1466	            Some(child) => {
  1467	                // Remove previous child from children list,
  1468	                // and add new child onto front of the list.
  1469	                let prev_child = self.replace_at_depth(context, child, depth);
  1470	                {
  1471	                    // Set initial properties for child.
  1472	                    child.set_instantiated_by_timeline(true);
  1473	                    child.set_depth(depth);
  1474	                    child.set_parent(context, Some(self.into()));
  1475	                    child.set_place_frame(self.current_frame());
  1476	
  1477	                    // If this MC hasn't had an `object2` allocated yet, this
  1478	                    // child will be constructed by `Sprite.constructChildren`,
  1479	                    // not by the timeline
  1480	                    let has_object2_allocated = self.object2().is_none();
  1481	                    child.set_manual_frame_construct(has_object2_allocated);
  1482	
  1483	                    // Apply PlaceObject parameters.
  1484	                    child.apply_place_object(context, place_object);
  1485	                    if let Some(name) = &place_object.name {
  1486	                        let encoding = swf::SwfStr::encoding_for_version(self.swf_version());
  1487	                        let name = AvmString::new(context.gc(), name.decode(encoding));
  1488	                        child.set_name(context.gc(), name);
  1489	                        child.set_has_explicit_name(true);
  1490	                    }
  1491	                    if let Some(clip_depth) = place_object.clip_depth {
  1492	                        child.set_clip_depth(clip_depth.into());
  1493	                    }
  1494	                    // Clip events only apply to movie clips.
  1495	                    if let (Some(clip_actions), Some(clip)) =
  1496	                        (&place_object.clip_actions, child.as_movie_clip())
  1497	                    {
  1498	                        // Convert from `swf::ClipAction` to Ruffle's `ClipEventHandler`.
  1499	                        clip.init_clip_event_handlers(
  1500	                            clip_actions
  1501	                                .iter()
  1502	                                .cloned()
  1503	                                .map(|a| ClipEventHandler::from_action_and_movie(a, movie.clone()))
  1504	                                .collect(),
  1505	                        );
  1506	                    }
  1507	                    // TODO: Missing PlaceObject property: amf_data
  1508	
  1509	                    // Run first frame.
  1510	                    child.post_instantiation(context, None, Instantiator::Movie, false);
  1511	                    child.enter_frame(context);
  1512	                    // In AVM1, children are added in `run_frame` so this is necessary.
  1513	                    // In AVM2 we add them in `construct_frame` so calling this causes
  1514	                    // duplicate frames
  1515	                    if let Some(child) = child.as_movie_clip()
  1516	                        && !movie.is_action_script_3()
  1517	                    {
  1518	                        child.run_frame_avm1(context);
  1519	                    }
  1520	                }
  1521	
  1522	                if let Some(prev_child) = prev_child {
  1523	                    dispatch_removed_event(prev_child, context);
  1524	                }
  1525	
  1526	                Some(child)
  1527	            }
  1528	            None => {
  1529	                tracing::error!("Unable to instantiate display node id {}", id,);
  1530	                None
  1531	            }
  1532	        }
  1533	    }

  2478	    fn enter_frame(self, context: &mut UpdateContext<'gc>) {
  2479	        let skip_frame = self.base().should_skip_next_enter_frame();
  2480	        //Child removals from looping gotos appear to resolve in reverse order.
  2481	        for child in self.iter_render_list().rev() {
  2482	            if skip_frame {
  2483	                // If we're skipping our current frame, then we want to skip it for our children
  2484	                // as well. This counts as the skipped frame for any children that already
  2485	                // has this set to true (e.g. a third-level grandchild doesn't skip three frames).
  2486	                // We'll still call 'enter_frame' on the child - it will recurse, propagating along
  2487	                // the flag, and then set its own flag back to 'false'.
  2488	                //
  2489	                // We do *not* propagate `skip_frame=false` down to children, since a normally
  2490	                // executing parent can add a child that should have its first frame skipped.
  2491	
  2492	                // FIXME - does this propagate through non-movie-clip children (Loader/Button)?
  2493	                child.base().set_skip_next_enter_frame(true);
  2494	            }
  2495	            child.enter_frame(context);
  2496	        }
  2497	
  2498	        if skip_frame {
  2499	            self.base().set_skip_next_enter_frame(false);
  2500	            return;
  2501	        }
  2502	
  2503	        if self.movie().is_action_script_3() {
  2504	            let is_playing = self.playing();
  2505	
  2506	            if is_playing {
  2507	                self.run_frame_internal(context, true, true, true);
  2508	            }
  2509	
  2510	            // PlaceObject tags execute at this time.
  2511	            // Note that this is NOT when constructors run; that happens later
  2512	            // after tags have executed.
  2513	            let data = self.0.shared.get().swf.clone();
  2514	            let place_actions = self.unqueue_filtered(|q| q.unqueue_add());
  2515	
  2516	            for (_, tag) in place_actions {
  2517	                let mut reader = data.read_from(tag.tag_start);
  2518	                let version = match tag.tag_type {
  2519	                    QueuedTagAction::Place(v) => v,
  2520	                    _ => unreachable!(),
  2521	                };
  2522	
  2523	                if let Err(e) = self.place_object(context, &mut reader, version) {
  2524	                    tracing::error!("Error running queued tag: {:?}, got {}", tag.tag_type, e);
  2525	                }

    80	/// - Changing the color transform
    81	/// - Any "visual" change to children, **including** position changes
    82	///
    83	/// Position changes to the cached Display Object does not regenerate the cache,
    84	/// allowing Display Objects to move freely without being regenerated.
    85	///
    86	/// Flash isn't very good at always recognising when it should be invalidated,
    87	/// and there's cases such as changing the blend mode which don't always trigger it.
    88	///
    89	#[derive(Clone, Debug, Default)]
    90	pub struct BitmapCache {
    91	    /// The `Matrix.a` value that was last used with this cache
    92	    matrix_a: f32,
    93	    /// The `Matrix.b` value that was last used with this cache
    94	    matrix_b: f32,
    95	    /// The `Matrix.c` value that was last used with this cache
    96	    matrix_c: f32,
    97	    /// The `Matrix.d` value that was last used with this cache
    98	    matrix_d: f32,
    99	
   100	    /// The width of the original bitmap, pre-filters
   101	    source_width: u32,
   102	
   103	    /// The height of the original bitmap, pre-filters
   104	    source_height: u32,
   105	
   106	    /// The offset used to draw the final bitmap (i.e. if a filter increases the size)
   107	    draw_offset: Point<i32>,
   108	
   109	    /// The current contents of the cache, if any. Values are post-filters.
   110	    bitmap: Option<BitmapInfo>,
   111	
   112	    /// Whether we warned that this bitmap was too large to be cached
   113	    warned_for_oversize: bool,
   114	}
   115	
   116	impl BitmapCache {
   117	    /// Forcefully make this BitmapCache invalid and require regeneration.
   118	    /// This should be used for changes that aren't automatically detected, such as children.
   119	    pub fn make_dirty(&mut self) {
   120	        // Setting the old transform to something invalid is a cheap way of making it invalid,
   121	        // without reserving an extra field for.
   122	        self.matrix_a = f32::NAN;
   123	    }
   124	
   125	    fn is_dirty(&self, other: &Matrix, source_width: u32, source_height: u32) -> bool {
   126	        self.matrix_a != other.a
   127	            || self.matrix_b != other.b
   128	            || self.matrix_c != other.c
   129	            || self.matrix_d != other.d
   130	            || self.source_width != source_width
   131	            || self.source_height != source_height
   132	            || self.bitmap.is_none()
   133	    }

   935	    this: DisplayObject<'gc>,
   936	    context: &mut RenderContext<'_, 'gc>,
   937	    options: RenderOptions,
   938	) {
   939	    if options.skip_masks && this.maskee().is_some() {
   940	        // Skip rendering masks (unless we are rendering one explicitly).
   941	        return;
   942	    }
   943	
   944	    if options.apply_transform {
   945	        let transform = this.base().transform(options.apply_matrix);
   946	        context.transform_stack.push(&transform);
   947	    }
   948	
   949	    let blend_mode = this.blend_mode();
   950	    let original_commands = if blend_mode != ExtendedBlendMode::Normal {
   951	        Some(std::mem::take(&mut context.commands))
   952	    } else {
   953	        None
   954	    };
   955	
   956	    let cache_info = if context.use_bitmap_cache && this.is_bitmap_cached() {
   957	        let mut cache_info: Option<DrawCacheInfo> = None;
   958	        let base_transform = context.transform_stack.transform();
   959	        let bounds: Rectangle<Twips> = this.render_bounds_with_transform(
   960	            &base_transform.matrix,
   961	            false, // we want to do the filter growth for this object ourselves, to know the offsets
   962	            &context.stage.view_matrix(),
   963	        );
   964	        let name = this.name();
   965	        let mut filters: Vec<Filter> = this.filters().to_owned();
   966	        let swf_version = this.swf_version();
   967	        filters.retain(|f| !f.impotent());
   968	
   969	        if let Some(cache) = &mut *this.base().bitmap_cache_mut() {
   970	            let width = bounds.width().to_pixels().ceil().max(0.0);
   971	            let height = bounds.height().to_pixels().ceil().max(0.0);
   972	            if width <= u16::MAX as f64 && height <= u16::MAX as f64 {
   973	                let width = width as u32;
   974	                let height = height as u32;
   975	                let mut filter_rect = Rectangle {
   976	                    x_min: Twips::ZERO,
   977	                    x_max: Twips::from_pixels_i32(width as i32),
   978	                    y_min: Twips::ZERO,
   979	                    y_max: Twips::from_pixels_i32(height as i32),
   980	                };
   981	                let stage_matrix = context.stage.view_matrix();
   982	                for filter in &mut filters {
   983	                    // Scaling is done by *stage view matrix* only, nothing in-between
   984	                    filter.scale(stage_matrix.a, stage_matrix.d);
   985	                    filter_rect = filter.calculate_dest_rect(filter_rect);
   986	                }
   987	                let filter_rect = Rectangle {
   988	                    x_min: filter_rect.x_min.to_pixels().floor() as i32,
   989	                    x_max: filter_rect.x_max.to_pixels().ceil() as i32,
   990	                    y_min: filter_rect.y_min.to_pixels().floor() as i32,

   522	    #[no_dynamic]
   523	    fn fill_tab_order(&self, tab_order: &mut TabOrder<'gc>, context: &mut UpdateContext<'gc>) {
   524	        if !self.is_tab_children(context) {
   525	            // AS3 docs say that objects with custom ordering (tabIndex set)
   526	            // are included even when tabChildren is false.
   527	            // Do not be fooled for that is untrue!
   528	            return;
   529	        }
   530	
   531	        for child in self.iter_render_list() {
   532	            if !child.visible() {
   533	                // Non-visible objects and their children are excluded from tab ordering.
   534	                continue;
   535	            }
   536	            if let Some(child) = child.as_interactive()
   537	                && child.is_tabbable(context)
   538	            {
   539	                tab_order.add_object(child);
   540	            }
   541	            if let Some(container) = child.as_container() {
   542	                container.fill_tab_order(tab_order, context);
   543	            }
   544	        }
   545	    }

   555	            child.pre_render(context);
   556	
   557	            // Check if we need to pop off a mask.
   558	            // This must be a while loop because multiple masks can be popped
   559	            // at the same depth.
   560	            while clip_depth > 0 && depth > clip_depth {
   561	                // Clear the mask stencil and pop the mask.
   562	                let (prev_clip_depth, clip_child) = clip_depth_stack.pop().unwrap();
   563	                clip_depth = prev_clip_depth;
   564	                context.commands.deactivate_mask();
   565	                clip_child.render(context);

    12	
    13	As best practice, please also include any source used to make the SWF, such as `test.fla` and/or any ActionScript files.
    14	
    15	# Test Structure
    16	
    17	## test.toml
    18	
    19	Except for `num_ticks`, every other field and section is optional.
    20	
    21	```toml
    22	# The number of frames of the SWF to run.
    23	num_ticks = 1
    24	
    25	# The number of milliseconds to process per tick.
    26	# By default this uses the SWF frame rate.
    27	tick_rate = 16.666
    28	
    29	# If true, sleep in between ticks to run at realtime speed.
    30	# Necessary for some timer tests.
    31	sleep_to_meet_frame_rate = false
    32	
    33	# If true, log AVM warnings.
    34	# Warnings are special AVM traces that can be produced by Flash Player (but
    35	# don't have to) and can provide insight into what AVM does.  This option can be
    36	# used to disable warnings in case the output does not contain them.
    37	log_warnings = true
    38	
    39	# If true, ignore this test.
    40	# Please comment why, ideally link to an issue, so we know what's up.
    41	# Prefer setting `known_failure = true` to ignoring the test.
    42	ignore = false
    43	
    44	# If specified, a cfg-like expression that checks if the test can run.
    45	# Useful for platform-specific tests.
    46	#
    47	# Available predicates:
    48	#  * os
    49	#  * arch
    50	#  * family
    51	filter = 'os = "windows"'
    52	
    53	# If true, this test is known to fail and the test runner will expect the check against
    54	# the trace output (specified `output_path`) to fail.
    55	# When the test passes in the future, it'll fail and alert that it now passes.
    56	# This will not catch Ruffle panics; if the test is expected to panic, use
    57	#   `known_failure.panic = "panic message"`
    58	# instead (note that 'panicky' tests will be skipped if the test harness is run
    59	# with debug assertions disabled, e.g. with `--release`).
    60	# By default, the test runner will additionally check Ruffle's output against itself
    61	# to detect regressions in failing tests; this can be disabled with
    62	#    `known_failure.ruffle_check = false`.
    63	known_failure = false
    64	
    65	# Path (relative to the directory containing test.toml) to the expected output
    66	output_path = "output.txt"

    68	# If true, all network requests will be included in the output.
    69	log_fetch = false
    70	
    71	# Sometimes floating point math doesn't exactly 100% match between Flash and Rust.
    72	# If you encounter this in a test, the following section will change the output

    74	[approximations]

    26	/// CLI options for running Ruffle tests, separate from cargo test's interface.
    27	#[derive(Parser, Debug, Clone)]
    28	struct RuffleTestOpts {
    29	    /// Ignore tests that are known to be failing
    30	    #[clap(long, action)]
    31	    ignore_known_failures: bool,
    32	}
    33	
    34	fn main() {
    35	    let _ = env_logger::Builder::from_env(
    36	        env_logger::Env::default().default_filter_or("info,wgpu_core=warn,wgpu_hal=warn"),
    37	    )
    38	    .format_timestamp(None)
    39	    .is_test(true)
    40	    .try_init();
    41	
    42	    let subscriber = tracing_subscriber::fmt::Subscriber::builder()
    43	        .with_env_filter(tracing_subscriber::EnvFilter::from_default_env())
    44	        .finish();
    45	    // Ignore error if it's already been set
    46	    let _ = tracing::subscriber::set_global_default(subscriber);
    47	
    48	    let ruffle_test_opts = match std::env::var("RUFFLE_TEST_OPTS") {
    49	        Ok(val) => val,
    50	        Err(std::env::VarError::NotPresent) => "".to_owned(),
    51	        e @ Err(_) => panic!("{e:?}"),
    52	    };
    53	    let ruffle_test_opts = RuffleTestOpts::parse_from(
    54	        // The first argument is the name of the executable, in our case pass
    55	        // the variable name in order to show the proper help message.
    56	        std::iter::once("RUFFLE_TEST_OPTS=")
    57	            .chain(ruffle_test_opts.split(" ").filter(|s| !s.is_empty())),
    58	    );
    59	
    60	    let mut runner = FsTestsRunner::new();
    61	
    62	    runner
    63	        .with_descriptor_name(Cow::Borrowed(TEST_TOML_NAME))
    64	        .with_root_dir(PathBuf::from("tests/swfs"))
    65	        .with_test_loader(Box::new(move |params, register_trial| {
    66	            for test in load_test_dir(&params.test_dir, params.test_name) {
    67	                let trial = trial_for_test(&ruffle_test_opts, test, params.args.list);
    68	                register_trial(trial);
    69	            }
    70	        }));
    71	
    72	    // Manual tests here, since #[test] doesn't work once we use our own test harness
    73	    runner.with_additional_test(Trial::test("shared_object_avm1", || {
    74	        shared_object_avm1(&NativeEnvironment)
    75	    }));
    76	    runner.with_additional_test(Trial::test("shared_object_self_ref_avm1", || {

    78	    }));
    79	    runner.with_additional_test(Trial::test("shared_object_avm2", || {
    80	        shared_object_avm2(&NativeEnvironment)
    81	    }));
    82	    runner.with_additional_test(Trial::test("external_interface_avm1", || {
    83	        external_interface_avm1(&NativeEnvironment)
    84	    }));
    85	    runner.with_additional_test(Trial::test("external_interface_avm2", || {
    86	        external_interface_avm2(&NativeEnvironment)
    87	    }));
    88	
    89	    runner.run()
    90	}
    91	
    92	fn load_test_dir<'a>(test_dir: &'a VfsPath, name: &'a str) -> impl Iterator<Item = Test> + 'a {
    93	    let options = TestOptions::read_with_subtests(&test_dir.join("test.toml").unwrap())
    94	        .with_context(|| format!("Couldn't load test options for test {name}"))
    95	        .unwrap();
    96	    options.into_iter().map(move |opts| {
    97	        Test::from_options(opts, test_dir.to_owned(), name.to_owned())
    98	            .with_context(|| format!("Couldn't create test {name}"))
    99	            .unwrap()
   100	    })
   101	}
   102	
   103	fn trial_for_test(opts: &RuffleTestOpts, test: Test, list_only: bool) -> Trial {
   104	    let ignore = !test.should_run(opts.ignore_known_failures, !list_only, &NativeEnvironment);
   105	
   106	    // Put extra info into the test 'kind' instead of appending it to the test name,
   107	    // to not break `cargo test some/test -- --exact` and `cargo test -- --list`.
   108	    let mut test_kind = String::new();
   109	    if test.options.has_known_failure() {
   110	        test_kind.push('!');
   111	    }
   112	    if let Some(name) = &test.options.subtest_name {
   113	        test_kind.push_str(name);
   114	    }
   115	
   116	    let trial = Trial::test(test.name.clone(), move || {
   117	        let mut runner = test.create_test_runner(&NativeEnvironment)?;
   118	
   119	        loop {
   120	            match runner.tick()? {
   121	                TestStatus::Continue => (),
   122	                TestStatus::Sleep(duration) => sleep(duration),
   123	                TestStatus::Finished => break Ok(()),
   124	            }
   125	        }
   126	    });
   127	
   128	    trial.with_ignored_flag(ignore).with_kind(test_kind)
   129	}
   130

+        .or_else(|| info.payload().downcast_ref::<String>().map(|s| s.as_str()))
+        .unwrap_or("panic occurred");
